#MySQL DUMP

#Table name: blockip

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS blockip;
CREATE TABLE `blockip` (
  `ip` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ip`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2;

#Table name: towns

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS towns;
CREATE TABLE `towns` (
  `xc` int(5) NOT NULL default '0',
  `yc` int(5) NOT NULL default '0',
  `obrazok` varchar(30) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default '0',
  `meno` varchar(50) collate latin2_czech_cs default NULL,
  `rand` int(1) NOT NULL default '1',
  `pozadie` varchar(30) collate latin2_czech_cs default NULL,
  `vlastnik` int(4) NOT NULL default '1',
  `cas` int(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `casovac` int(11) default NULL,
  `napis` text collate latin2_czech_cs,
  `uroven` int(9) NOT NULL default '1',
  `budovanas` text collate latin2_czech_cs,
  `zivot` int(9) NOT NULL,
  `utokna` int(9) NOT NULL default '0',
  UNIQUE KEY `xcyc` (`xc`,`yc`),
  KEY `vlastnik` (`vlastnik`),
  KEY `obrazok` (`obrazok`),
  KEY `cas` (`cas`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2 COLLATE=latin2_czech_cs;

#Table name: townsali

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS townsali;
CREATE TABLE `townsali` (
  `id` int(9) NOT NULL default '0',
  `meno` varchar(20) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default '',
  `body` int(9) default NULL,
  `poradie` int(9) default NULL,
  `popis` text collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `body` (`body`),
  KEY `meno` (`meno`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2 COLLATE=latin2_czech_cs;

#Table name: townsalidis

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS townsalidis;
CREATE TABLE `townsalidis` (
  `id` int(9) NOT NULL default '0',
  `ali` int(9) NOT NULL default '0',
  `nadpis` varchar(20) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default '',
  `meno` int(9) NOT NULL default '0',
  `text` text collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2 COLLATE=latin2_czech_cs;

#Table name: townsank

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS townsank;
CREATE TABLE `townsank` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `autor` int(9) NOT NULL,
  `schvaleno` int(1) NOT NULL,
  `otazka` text,
  `hraci` text,
  `o1` text,
  `p1` int(9) default '0',
  `o2` text,
  `p2` int(9) default '0',
  `o3` text,
  `p3` int(9) default '0',
  `o4` text,
  `p4` int(9) default '0',
  `o5` text,
  `p5` int(9) default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2;

#Table name: townsdis

  `cas` timestamp NOT NULL default CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2 COLLATE=latin2_czech_cs;

#Table name: townskod

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS townskod;
CREATE TABLE `townskod` (
  `kod` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `prachy` bigint(9) NOT NULL,
  `seria` int(9) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`kod`),
  KEY `seria` (`seria`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2;

#Table name: townsld

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS townsld;
CREATE TABLE `townsld` (
  `hrac` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `co` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `prachy` int(11) NOT NULL,
  UNIQUE KEY `hrac` (`hrac`,`co`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2;


#DATA



#Table name: townsmes

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS townsmes;
CREATE TABLE `townsmes` (
  `id` int(4) NOT NULL default '0',
  `meno` varchar(20) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default '',
  `popis` text collate latin2_czech_cs,
  `body` int(10) default NULL,
  `poradie` int(9) NOT NULL,
  `hlbudovaxc` int(4) default NULL,
  `hlbudovayc` int(4) default NULL,
  `prachy` int(9) default NULL,
  `jedlo` int(9) default NULL,
  `kamen` int(9) default NULL,
  `zelezo` int(9) default NULL,
  `drevo` int(9) default NULL,
  `ludia` int(9) NOT NULL,
  `ludiamax` int(9) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `body` (`body`),
  KEY `meno` (`meno`),
  KEY `poradie` (`poradie`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2 COLLATE=latin2_czech_cs;

#Table name: townssta

  `id` int(9) NOT NULL default '0',

#Table name: townsuni

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS townsuni;
CREATE TABLE `townsuni` (
  `meno` varchar(20) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default 'beze jména',
  `popis` text collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL,
  `stavanie` text collate latin2_czech_cs,
  `casovac2` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `obrazok` varchar(20) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default '',
  `akce` varchar(20) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default 'postavit budovu',
  `drevo` int(4) NOT NULL default '0',
  `kamen` int(4) NOT NULL default '0',
  `jedlo` int(9) default NULL,
  `zivot` varchar(4) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default '10',
  `utok` char(2) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default '0',
  `vutok` int(2) NOT NULL default '1',
  `ludia` int(1) NOT NULL default '1',
  `pludia` int(2) NOT NULL default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`meno`),
  UNIQUE KEY `obrazok` (`obrazok`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2 COLLATE=latin2_czech_cs;

#Table name: townsutok

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS townsutok;
CREATE TABLE `townsutok` (
  `id` int(6) NOT NULL default '0',
  `cas` int(11) NOT NULL default '1',
  `xc` int(4) default NULL,
  `yc` int(4) default NULL,
  `xczo` int(4) default NULL,
  `yczo` int(4) default NULL,
  `xc2` int(4) default NULL,
  `yc2` int(4) default NULL,
  `vojak` text collate latin2_czech_cs,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `xc2` (`xc2`),
  KEY `yc2` (`yc2`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2 COLLATE=latin2_czech_cs;

#Table name: townsuziv

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS townsuziv;
CREATE TABLE `townsuziv` (
  `id` int(3) NOT NULL default '0',
  `typ` int(1) NOT NULL,
  `meno` varchar(20) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default '',
  `ali` int(9) NOT NULL,
  `body` int(9) default NULL,
  `poradie` int(9) NOT NULL,
  `heslo` text collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL,
  `popis` text collate latin2_czech_cs,
  `pohlavie` int(1) default NULL,
  `vek` int(2) default NULL,
  `mail` varchar(50) collate latin2_czech_cs default NULL,
  `zmail` int(1) default NULL,
  `www` varchar(50) collate latin2_czech_cs default NULL,
  `mestozal` int(9) NOT NULL,
  `lista` text collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL,
  `aktivita` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `meno` (`meno`),
  KEY `body` (`body`),
  KEY `poradie` (`poradie`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2 COLLATE=latin2_czech_cs;

#Table name: townszpr

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS townszpr;
CREATE TABLE `townszpr` (
  `id` int(9) NOT NULL default '0',
  `od` int(9) NOT NULL default '0',
  `komu` int(9) NOT NULL default '0',
  `precitane` int(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `cas` timestamp NOT NULL default CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `predmet` varchar(20) collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL default '',
  `zprava` text collate latin2_czech_cs NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `idx_komu` (`komu`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2 COLLATE=latin2_czech_cs;
